Oral CD11b Modulator for Solid Tumor Oncology Indications</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.8pt">Enrollment ongoing in a Phase 1 expansion cohort studying the recommended Phase 2 dose in KEYNOTE-A36, a Phase 1&#47;2 clinical trial, including patients with gastric or esophageal cancer who have progressed after initial response to anti-PD-1 therapy and patients with advanced MSS colorectal cancer. </font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.13pt">Additional clinical data from the ongoing GB1275 Phase 1&#47;2 will be presented at the American Society of Clinical Oncology (ASCO) 2021 Annual Meeting being held virtually from June 4 - 8, 2021. Cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities as of March 31, 2021, were $453.3 million. The Company expects the combination of current cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities, and access to its debt facility will be sufficient to fund its operating and capital expenditures into the second half of 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.13pt">Research and Development (R&#38;D) Expenses</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#58; For the quarter ended March 31, 2021, R&#38;D expenses were $41.8 million, compared to R&#38;D expenses of $41.4 million for the same period in 2020. </font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">General and Administrative (G&#38;A) Expenses</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#58; For the quarter ended March 31, 2021, G&#38;A expenses were $11.3 million, compared to $10.7 million for the same period in 2020. </font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Net Loss</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#58; Net loss for the quarter ended March 31, 2021, was $57.6 million, or $0.78 per share, compared to a net loss of $54.1 million, or $0.87 per share, for the same period in 2020.  </font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">About&#160;Gossamer Bio</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gossamer Bio is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on discovering, acquiring, developing and commercializing therapeutics in the disease areas of immunology, inflammation and oncology. Its goal is to be an industry leader in each of these therapeutic areas and to enhance and extend the lives of patients suffering from such diseases.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gossamer cautions you that statements contained in this press release regarding matters that are not historical facts are forward-looking statements. These statements are based on the Company&#8217;s current beliefs and expectations. Such forward-looking statements include, but are not limited to, statements regarding&#58; the anticipated timing of enrollment of clinical trials for our product candidates&#59; plans to advance our product candidates&#59; expectations on the timing of data readouts from our clinical studies&#59; the expected impact of COVID-19&#59; and the expected timeframe for funding our operating plan with current cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities.
